I'm so sorry for the inconvenience and truly appreciate your patience as we work to address this.
There are still issues with test mode and we are actively working to improve its stability. In many cases, ending the session and retrying or simply waiting for a bit tends to help the issue.
We're hoping our latest release (6.1.11) resolves some of these issues, but please note the load time is known to take longer.
We will continue improving this experience, and I would also like to recommend our "Local Run" feature, which runs the project locally on a simulator (Local Run Documentation). After getting setup, your project can remain running for much longer periods of time and you can use hot-reload with Local Run as well.

5. –û—Å–æ–±–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å FlutterFlow
